## [CHARACTERS] Ewig the Sage
**Ewig the Sage** ｢賢 (けん) 者 (じゃ) エーヴィヒ, *Kenja Ēvihi*?｣ was a human Sage from the Mythical Era and an exceptional mage who propelled forward humanity's knowledge of magic. He was the creator of the Stone Bracelet of Servitude.

## Personality]

Not much is known about Ewig's personality. However, his studies in magic hint at his curious mind and his endeavors towards the betterment of society, as he recorded the knowledge he gained in grimoires. His creation of the Stone Bracelet of Servitude is also a reflection of his inventiveness.

## Appearance]

Ewig the Sage was of a typical human stature. His hair was long, dark, and wavy, and it flowed down to his lower back. He wore a simple, long robe that reached the ground. He wore another garment layer underneath his robe, which was bound with a sash. Over his robe, Ewig wore a short, cloak-like cape with a fringe layer along the hem. As a mage, he wielded a straight staff with a curved top that had a gem in the center.

## Synopsis]

### History]

Ewig the Sage was a mage from the Mythical Era whose grimoires supposedly contained secrets about immortality and resurrection. He coded his grimoires with images. At some point, Ewig recorded his knowledge of the water-mirror demon, the Spiegel, into his adventuring tales.

### Beyond Journey's End Arc]

Twenty years after the death of Himmel the Hero, Frieren visits Heiter, where she gets presented a grimoire written by Ewig the Sage that was excavated from the sage's grave. Heiter explains that the grimoire is said to contain long-lost spells of resurrection and immortality. Frieren disbelieves this claim, but she is willing to decipher it for Heiter, and she estimates the task will take approximately five to six years as people from back then were fond of image ciphers. 

After a few years go by, Frieren finishes deciphering the grimoire and presents Heiter with the notes on his deathbed. With her findings, she reveals that no spells for resurrection and immortality were recorded in the book. Heiter tells the elf that if such a thing existed, Ewig himself would have used it, as fear of death is immeasurable. He reveals that the deciphering was an excuse to trick Frieren into training Fern so the young mage would not be a burden as an apprentice.

### First-Class Mage Exam Arc]

Twenty-nine years after the death of Himmel the Hero, during the second stage of the First-Class Mage Exam, proctors Genau and Falsch converse about proctor Sense's choice of the Ruins of the King's Tomb as a test location. Genau tells Falsch that the Spiegel, a water-mirror demon and the lord of the dungeon, is a monster from the mythical times and appears in Ewig's heroic tales.

### The Golden Land Arc]

Thirty years after the death of Himmel the Hero, first-class mage Lernen approaches the second-class mage Edel for aid on a mission. He explains that he is trying to help his friend Denken, and he requests for Edel to help him investigate the Stone Bracelet of Servitude—the only item in the world which can control the mind of a demon—because she is highly skilled in hypnosis magic. Lernen discloses that he believed the item malfunctioned, as the demon Macht, who had to wear the bracelet by the order of the people in the city of Weise, was ultimately able to curse the Golden Land. He shows Edel a faithfully recreated replica and asks her to analyze the hypnosis spell placed on it, as the original bracelet was reportedly still being worn by Macht. 

After confronting Macht and investigating the real bracelet firsthand, Edel verifies to Lernen that the Stone Bracelet of Servitude has always functioned correctly and the hypnosis magic had not lost its effect. She also reveals that only the original user can add another command to it.

## Abilities]

- **Hypnosis magic** ｢精 (せい) 神 (しん) 操 (そう) 作 (さ) 魔 (ま) 法 (ほう) , *Seishin sōsa mahō*?｣: Ewig was capable of hypnosis magic, as he created the Stone Bracelet of Servitude, a bracelet with a hypnosis spell cast on it that allowed individuals to give a command to the wearer and force them to obey. Notably, this bracelet was the only magical item known to be able to manipulate a demon's mind. Despite being created so long ago, Edel confirms that the Stone Bracelet of Servitude placed on Macht of the Golden Land is still functioning properly.

## [CHARACTERS] Falsch
IntroductionGallery

**Falsch** ｢ファルシュ, *Farushu*?｣ is a first-class mage. He gauges the candidates with Sense for the First-Class Mage Exam on the sidelines before the first stage begins and is the one to announce the format of the third stage of the exam.

## Personality]

Falsch is an observant and perceptive first-class mage, demonstrated by his keen analysis of the exam candidates and their backgrounds. He is confident in his abilities and assessments, possessing a deep understanding of mana manipulation, even though he is not always correct, as shown when he fails to notice Frieren's mana suppression.

Falsch remains composed even in the face of setbacks, such as after the capture of Übel and Land by the Magic Special Forces. He prefers to wait and observe rather than rush into action, and serves as the voice of reason when Sense proposes reckless endeavors. His maturity is further evident in his exasperation at the hostilities between Lineal and Sense. He is also skilled domestically and rises early to cook and make sure his fellow first-class mage Sense is appropriately prepared for the day.

## Appearance]

Falsch is a human mage of tall stature. He has short, slicked back dark hair, with two long strands flowing loosely over his forehead. He wears round glasses, and like the other first-class mages his attire features the color dark blue prominently. Falsch wears a predominantly dark blue robe, with gray lining and an upturned collar, paired with a short cape that drapes over his shoulders.

## Synopsis]

At some point prior to Übel's attempt at the Second-Class Mage Exam, Falsch passes the First-Class Mage Exam and becomes a first-class mage. He becomes one of Serie's apprentices in Äußerst. 

Falsch is present along with fellow first-class mage Sense during the second stage of the Second-Class Mage Exam proctored by Burg. He reads a book throughout the second stage, and appears mildly surprised when Übel manages to kill Burg.

### First-Class Mage Exam Arc (First Stage)]

Before the first stage of the First-Class Mage Exam begins, Falsch and Sense stand to the side in the exam hall and observe the pool of candidates. Falsch remarks that the quality of the candidates this year appears to be pretty good. In particular, he points out Wirbel, Captain of the Northern Magic Corps, Denken, the imperial mage, and Fern, the youngest mage to pass the third-class exam with the highest score. Falsch then pushes up his glasses and remarks that they have a troublemaker in their midst as well—Übel. Falsch continues to assess which candidates are promising, and his attention is drawn by Frieren, who he notes has the mana of an old, experienced mage. He asks Sense who that mage is but Sense also has no idea, and they are distracted by Genau announcing the start of the first stage of the exam.

### First-Class Mage Exam Arc (Second Stage)]

While Sense conducts the second stage of the First-Class Mage Exam, Falsch is seen having tea with Genau in a library of the Continental Magic Association. After Genau explains why the Ruins of the King's Tomb has thus far been impregnable, Falsch questions why Sense would choose the dungeon as the location of the second stage of the exam.

### First-Class Mage Exam Arc (Final Stage)]

Before the third stage of the First-Class Mage Exam, Serie arrives and gathers all the first-class mages in her room in the Continental Magic Association. Lernen tells Serie that he is unqualified to test Frieren, as he was able to tell at a glance that Frieren was suppressing her mana. Serie then asks Falsch whether he noticed this as well, to which Falsch replies negatively. Falsch states that he saw Frieren's mana in the exam hall with his own eyes, and that there was no sign of the instability that occurs whenever mana is restrained. He demonstrates this by restraining his own mana and showing the resultant instability. Falsch then concludes that even if it were possible, to eliminate this instability, one would have to spend an unimaginable amount of time working on mana restraint, rendering it an unpractical technique. Serie tells the other first-class mages that Frieren is one that has devoted her whole life to said unpractical technique.

Later, Falsch is the one to announce the format of the third stage to the remaining first-class mage candidates. He tells the mages that have gathered in front of the doors of the exam hall that the third stage will be an interview with the Great Mage Serie.

### Foundation Festival Arc]

During the National Foundation Festival, Falsch and Sense are assigned to protect Serie after First-Class Mage Lineal warns them of an assassination plot targeting her during the grand ball in the Imperial Capital, Eiseberg.

In the capital, Falsch and Sense await the arrival of Frieren's party and seek their assistance. As Sense outlines the mission, Fern asks about the other two First-Class Mages involved. Falsch explains that Übel and Land are currently gathering vital intelligence.

Later that day, after Übel and Land were captured by the Empire’s Magic Special Forces, Falsch and Sense discuss the situation and wonder what the Special Forces might be doing here in the capital. Eventually, Sense decides that she will bail out both Übel and Land, though Falsch advises against this, noting the Special Forces' resentment towards Sense and their familiarity with her. Falsch recommends that they should wait it out.

The next day, Falsch prepares breakfast for the group, including Fern, Stark, Frieren, and Sense. While pouring a drink for Sense, he chides her for reading during the meal. After breakfast, Frieren, Fern, and Stark go to the market and buy a vase from the era of the Unified Empire. Upon their return, Falsch examines the vase and confirms it is a fake, which causes Frieren to fall down and cry. Later, as Frieren sulks, Falsch is seen examining a map for the upcoming operation.

After the Shadow Warriors conclude their meeting, Falsch secretly watches Routine and Iris from behind a pillar as they leave through an underground passage.

*This section is currently in active development. This article is expected to be high-traffic among editors, which can result in frequent changes. This may be due to its relevance in ongoing arcs or editors focusing on developing certain pages.*
*Feel free to help Frieren Wiki by **expanding it**. Please be sure to adhere to the Editor's Guidelines, Manual of Style, and Image Policy.*

## Abilities]

Falsch is a strong mage, as indicated by his status as a first-class mage. He is one of the three mages pictured, alongside Sense and Genau, when Richter extols the inhuman power of first-class mages.

- **Mana detection:** Falsch is shown to be skilled at mana detection. Before the first stage of the First-Class Mage Exam, he is able to clearly discern the mana output of the candidates and point out which candidates are most promising. However, unlike Lernen, Falsch is unable to detect the fluctuations of Frieren's restrained mana output.

- **Hand-to-hand combat:** As stated by Sense, both she and Falsch excel in hand-to-hand combat, and they are on the level of skilled Warriors. This suggests that Falsch's magic grants him powerful close-quarters capabilities similar to Sense's hair magic.

### Spells]

- **Unnamed shadow magic**: Falsch can conceal himself in a shadow and seemingly emerge at will. He also appears to be capable of manipulating the shadows around him.

- **Unnamed cloaking magic**: Falsch can cast a spell that envelops a target in a cloak, which he uses on Serie to keep her hidden.

- **Spell to change his voice freely**: After passing the First-Class Mage Exam, Falsch requested a voice changing spell from Serie. The spell allows Falsch to mimic the voice of any person he desires, and he specifically requested the spell to enable him to reproduce Serie's voice.

## [CHARACTERS] Fass
“
If you're gonna drink, you might as well enjoy it, eh?—Fass, in Chapter 69

IntroductionGallery

**Fass** ｢ファス, *Fasu*?｣ is a dwarf that lives in the Bier Region. He dedicated his life towards searching for the spirit named "Boshaft," having spent over two centuries looking for it.

## Personality]

Fass is very passionate about alcohol. He has eagerly dedicated two centuries of his life in search of an alcoholic drink and is willing to spend copious amounts of money and learn new skills in an effort to find the finest spirit. Fass is also good natured and positive. He gets along well with the townspeople and does not hesitate to share Boshaft once he finally finds it. Despite Frieren's fears that Fass would grow dispirited from learning his life's ambition had been for a spirit that was not actually good, Fass is cheerful upon finally trying Boshaft for himself and laughs about how awful it is. He immediately gathers all the townspeople to try the drink with him.

## Appearance]

Fass is, as all dwarves are, very small. He has darker hair that he wears a worn out top hat on top of and a bushy, disheveled beard. His attire consists of a white shirt tied at the waist with a thick black belt. The belt also holds his dark colored pants. He wears a baggy, oversized jacket on top of the rest of his attire.

## Synopsis]

### History]

Fass was born over two centuries ago in a town.

Eighty years ago, on their adventure to defeat the Demon King, the Hero Party met Fass. He asked them to help him with his goal to find the spirit "Boshaft," and although Heiter really wanted to assist, the Hero Party were forced to decline and move on with their quest. 

### Continued Northern Travels Arc]

Twenty-nine years after the death of Himmel the Hero, Frieren's Party visit the Bier Region and encounter Fass, who has progressed significantly in his quest for the spirit Boshaft. Fass tells them about the legend of Boshaft being buried in ruins in the area, which he came to strongly believe in when he found the stone monument carved by Milliarde. 

Fass explains to them that he learned how to mine in service of finding Boshaft, and leads them down the mine to the stone door at the end of the ruins. While he leads them, he explains that while dwarves are often associated with mines, he grew up in a town and thus he had to teach himself mining skills in order to dig the mine to reach Boshaft. He then asks Frieren to decipher the barrier barring access to the room behind the door, as Boshaft lies behind the door. When Frieren refuses, citing Fern and Stark's impatience, he offers to pay Frieren twenty Reich gold coins. When Frieren still declines, he then pleads with her, as it has been his dream to drink Boshaft and he has been searching for over two centuries. 

Once Frieren finally agrees, he spends the next three months assisting them where he can and spending time with Frieren, Fern, and Stark when they are not deciphering the barrier. After Frieren finally dispels the barrier, he remarks on how well Boshaft has been preserved, before taking a big swig of it. He appears at a loss for words, and Frieren interjects and calls the drink awful. When he sees Frieren, Fern, and Stark all laughing over how bad the drink tastes, he agrees with the taste, before bursting into laughter at the amount of bottles in the room, and telling the party to bring the whole town to try it. The townspeople all gather and try Boshaft, and as Fass sees the party off, he tells them that while the outcome was disappointing, he has never had as fun a night and he is glad they were there to try Boshaft with him.

## [TECHNIQUES] Golem Magic
**Golem magic** is a form of magic centered around creating golems for combat and support usage. The appearances and traits of these golems are dependent on the caster.

## Overview]

Golem magic has been known to mankind since over a millenium ago and since at least the Unified Empire era, where it was commonly utilized for military purposes. During this period, the Great Mage Flamme created a cooking golem that still functions in present day.

The golems created by mages through this magic can vary in construction, size, and capabilities, depending on the purpose of the golem and possibly the mage's proficiency at golem magic. The golems can be commanded with spells and function autonomously. Golems emit mana that is different from the mana emitted by monsters.

## Usage]

Golems can serve varying purposes depending on the intention of the caster, and they can achieve feats such as movement, spellcasting, and defense.

### Puppet Golems]

Frieren can create puppet golems using her **spell that manipulates stones as puppets** ｢石 (いし) を人 (にん) 形 (ぎょう) のように操 (あやつ) る魔 (ま) 法 (ほう) , *Ishi o ningyō no yō ni ayatsuru mahō*?｣. She constructs these golems by attaching stones together, creating a roughly anthropomorphic figure, and she can manipulate their movements.

When Frieren talks to Stark about defeating the Solar Dragon, she recalls a past instance of her using the spell to create a dancing golem as entertainment for the Hero Party.

During Frieren's battle against her Spiegel clone in the Ruins of the King's Tomb, she also uses this spell to create a massive golem from the debris in the room, which she lands on to gain the high ground. The golem mirrors her offensive and defensive spells.

A version of this spell is also seen being used by two children to entertain themselves in Eiseberg during the Foundation Festival.

### Bottled Golems]

First-class mage Lernen utilizes golem magic to create bottled versions of his golems. By shrinking the golems and placing them in bottles, he is able to effectively transport and share them among other individuals.

#### Escape Golems]

During the second stage of the First-Class Mage Exam, located at the Ruins of the King's Tomb, Lernen designed a prototype of an **escape golem** ｢脱 (だっ) 出 (しゅつ) 用 (よう) ゴーレム, *Dasshutsuyō gōremu*?｣ for examinees to use. These golems are a form of his bottled golems, and Sense instructs the candidates to use them in the event of an emergency. 

The bottles provide convenient transport of the golems, and they can be released and expanded to their original forms upon shattering the bottles. The golems are sturdy with muscular frames and react swiftly when released. They are able to forcefully evacuate even incapacitated users out of dangerous zones to a previously defined location while simultaneously defending against threats. The golems are strong enough to break through walls and can use healing magic if the user is injured.

#### Combat Golems]

When Lernen and Edel face Macht, Lernen breaks a bottle containing a combat golem as a distraction against Macht. The combat golem is a massive golem that wears armor and wields a sword, and it is swift and possesses enormous strength.

### Cooking Golem]

The Great Mage Flamme created a **cooking golem** ｢調 (ちょう) 理 (り) 用 (よう) ゴーレム, *Chōriyō gōremu*?｣ during the Unified Empire era. It has a tall, arthropodic appearance with a long, curved, and segmented body and four arms with a basket on its back. Its head is round and has a large, circular eye. The golem is sturdy and harder than metal. If a meal is requested, it will collect the necessary ingredients autonomously. A spell needs to be cast to deactivate the golem.

### Military Golems]

**Military golem** ｢軍 (ぐん) 用 (よう) ゴーレム, *Gunyō gōremu*?｣ are golems created for military use. They were used as weapons during the Unified Empire era.

## Gallery]

Fern holds a bottled escape golem.An escape golem heals Richter's injury.Lernen summons a combat golem in his fight against Macht.

## [TECHNIQUES] Zoltraak
**Zoltraak** ｢一般攻撃魔法 (ゾルトラーク) , *Zorutorāku*?｣, alternatively known as **killing magic** ｢人を殺す魔法 (ゾルトラーク) , ***killing magic***?｣, **demon-killing magic** ｢魔族を殺す魔法 (ゾルトラーク) , ***demon-killing magic***?｣, or, in modern day, **ordinary offensive magic** ｢一 (いっ) 般 (ぱん) 攻 (こう) 撃 (げき) 魔 (ま) 法 (ほう) , *Ippan kōgeki mahō*?｣, is a piercing spell that was originally developed by the demon Qual. The spell was later researched by humans and incorporated into their magic system, ultimately becoming a form of ordinary offensive magic that is used by modern mages.

## Overview]

Zoltraak was originally developed as a killing spell by the Elder Sage of Corruption, Qual, a member of the Demon King's army. The spell was known as the first piercing spell, and at the time, it was capable of piercing through humanity's defensive magic and magic-resistant equipment, directly devastating the individuals it struck. Eighty years prior to his death, Qual committed many atrocities in the region surrounding the Größe Forest with this spell, wiping out 40 percent of adventurers and 70 percent of mages in said region. 

Frieren of the Hero Party ultimately sealed Qual on the Hero Party's journey to defeat the Demon King. After Qual was petrified, mages across the continent began studying Zoltraak and eventually managed to incorporate it into the human magic system after a few years, with research of the spell spanning half a century. With the principles behind Zoltraak unraveled, new and powerful defensive spells and equipment were designed to counteract it. Additionally, Frieren, one of the major contributors towards this research, modified Zoltraak into a variant effective against demons—demon-killing magic—that she later taught to Fern. She unseals Qual when traveling with Fern and ultimately kills him with his own spell. Solitär implies that Zoltraak was used by humans to kill during the war in the Southern Lands, becoming the war's most lethal spell.

Due to how recently Zoltraak was assimilated into the present-day magic system, individuals born after the spell was integrated have learned to block it reflexively, as the spell is considered a fundamental element of their magic training. This poses an advantage against older mages, such as elves like Frieren or certain demons, as their experience with the spell in proportion to their ages means they have slightly delayed reactions defending against it.

## Usage]

Zoltraak is a simple spell that involves a blast of concentrated mana, either as a single shot or a saturation attack consisting of a barrage of Zoltraak casts. The size of the blast and the concentration or density of mana within a Zoltraak cast are adjustable, with highly concentrated spells appearing to be more powerful, though maintaining the speed is a difficult feat. When mages cast Zoltraak, they typically use a staff to direct the attack, but in some cases, they can cast the spell directly from their hand. A magic circle with a six-petaled flower indicates when Zoltraak is about to be cast.

Mages that are adept at casting magic quickly, such as Fern, can overwhelm opponents with a rapid-fire barrage of Zoltraak shots and prevent them from acquiring an opening. Additionally, these mages can cast a highly-concentrated Zoltraak from a distance to do damage while avoiding detection.

## Gallery]

Qual casts a barrage of his original killing magic variant of Zoltraak.Lügner is struck by a concentrated Zoltraak blast after failing to detect Fern.Fern strikes Solitär with Zoltraak from afar.The Zoltraak magic circle.

## Trivia]

- The original version of Zoltraak—killing magic—is represented in the anime as a black blast of mana, while the other forms of Zoltraak are represented with white blasts.

- There appears to be multiple variations of the Zoltraak magic circle, such as a version with a star instead of a six-petaled flower in Chapter 5. However, the six-petaled flower is the most frequently seen version.

- Fern has been depicted with mana butterflies when casting Zoltraak.

## [LOCATIONS] Alt Woods
The **Alt Woods** ｢アルト森 (しん) 林 (りん) , *Aruto Shinrin*?｣ is a forest past the Appetit Region in the Northern Lands. It is the location of Sein and his brother's hometown.

## Overview]

### Terrain and Ecology]

The Alt Woods is a densely forested region with hills, rivers, and bottomless swamps. Various herbs in the woods can be foraged. The rivers are home to fish, while the woods are filled with wild fruits and herbs. The locality is shown to have farmlands used to produce abundant crops. As with most places in the Northern Lands, travelers may encounter dangerous creatures. Most notably, venomous creatures are present in the area. These include venomous snakes, one of which bites Stark and releases venom that can only be cured in the early stages.

### Village]

A small and modest village with some farmlands and a river is located within the Alt Woods, and it is Sein and his brother's hometown. Warrior Gorilla once lived in the village, but he set out ten years prior to adventure around the Northern Lands. In the autumn, the town holds a harvest festival.

## Synopsis]

### History]

Sein, his brother, and Gorilla grew up in the village in the Alt Woods. At some point early in their childhood, Sein and his brother's parents passed away. Sein's brother would take on the responsibility of caring for his brother. Both Sein and Gorilla had dreams of leaving the village and adventuring. They would often play rambunctiously in the village, and Sein would often share these dreams with his brother. When they were younger, a traveling mage visited the village and took a picture of Sein and Gorilla together using photo-taking magic. It is unknown when Sein and his brother began their work in the clergy, but they both grew up to be skilled with the Goddess's Magic.

Heiter visited the village while Sein was younger in an official capacity from the Holy City of Strahl. He conducted inspections of the church and assessed Sein's brother to be the best priest in the region and conferred upon him a Holy Symbol. He additionally invited Sein's brother to work in the Holy City, but Sein's brother refused, as he was fine with his life in the village and did not want to take Sein's hometown away from him. Sein overhears this and begins to feel guilty for the perceived sacrifice his brother made for him.

Ten years prior to Frieren's Party's visit to the village, Gorilla decided to go out and travel in the Northern Lands. He asked Sein to come with him, as they had both wanted to adventure since childhood. However, Sein refused him, and Gorilla stated that he will return in three years' time for the village's annual harvest festival. However, ten years go by without word from Gorilla, and Sein began to believe he was dead.

### Travels to Äußerst Arc]

Twenty-nine years after Himmel's death, Frieren encounters Sein stuck in a swamp while she is gathering herbs. He tells her his ambition of becoming an adventurer, remembering in a flashback the time when his friend, Warrior Gorilla, tried to take him on an adventure. When Fern appears, Frieren remembers a spell to pull someone out of a bottomless swamp. Frieren's Party part ways with Sein near his village, and he warns them about the venomous animals in the forest. Shortly after that, Stark is bitten by a venomous snake. To get Stark cured, Frieren and Fern bring him to Sein's village. They visit the local church and meet Sein, who, as a priest, can treat the snake bite.

After seeing Sein's competency with the Goddess's Magic, Frieren is determined that Sein has to join her party. Stark attempts to convince Sein to join by visiting him in a bar. They both place bets, and Sein says he will join the party if Stark wins. However, the village chief wins the gamble and takes it all, leaving them humiliated in their underwear, and they receive help from Fern and Frieren. At that, Frieren remembers in a flashback how Himmel once convinced her to join the Hero Party.

The next days Frieren's party helps out in the village with various tasks while the harvest festival takes place. Sein rejects all attempts to convince him and declares he does not want to join the party. Frieren's party visits Sein's brother in the church to think of other approaches. Sein's brother tells them that Sein likes older ladies, prompting the idea to introduce Sein to an older lady: Frieren. Outside, Frieren attempts to flirt with Sein by using her master's secret technique: blowing him a kiss. It fails, which surprises Frieren, as she remembered how well Himmel was taken aback when she tried the technique on him. Sein repeats his intent to not become an adventurer. He reasons that he wishes not to leave his brother alone because his brother stayed in the village for him. Upon hearing this, Sein's brother is full of indignation, and he slaps Sein and tells him that he did not regret his choice to stay. He demands Sein to overthink his regrets. At last convinced, Sein decides to become an adventurer and joins the party on their journey to Aureole, with his goal being to find Gorilla.

## [LOCATIONS] Appetit Region
The **Appetit Region** ｢アぺティート地 (ち) 方 (ほう) , *Apetīto Chihō*?｣ is a mountainous region in the Northern Lands. It features snowy terrain, forests, and a town.

## Overview]

### Terrain and Ecology]

The Appetit Region has mountainous terrain, and its high altitude contributes to long winters and cold weather with regular snowfall. The vegetation is sparse, but coniferous trees grow within lush forests in the location. Human occupation is secluded and secured against dangerous wildlife. Domesticated cats and dogs are present, and cattle is raised. As with most places in the Northern Lands, travelers may encounter dangerous creatures.

### The Town]

A town in the Appetit Region houses a sizable population and contains many establishments. The buildings within the town appear to be built with primarily wood and stone.

## Synopsis]

### Travels to Äußerst Arc]

Twenty-nine years after Himmel's death, on Stark's eighteenth birthday, Frieren and Fern discuss what to give him as birthday gifts. Frieren decides on a potion that melts clothes, which is quickly shut down by Fern, who pours it on her, leaving Frieren to find a new gift. For that, she combs once more through her suitcase.

Fern decides to investigate Stark on her own. She tracks his deeds done through the town and ends up meeting him. She then asks him directly what he desires. Stark mentions how he never received gifts growing up due to his weakness, and his brother, Stoltz, the best warrior in his hometown and the only one kind to Stark, was the one to fight against demons during an attack while he simply fled. Fern comforts him and they find a gift, a bracelet, that Stark chooses.

Stark and Fern return to the inn where Frieren is cooking giant hamburger steaks. Frieren reveals she received the recipe from Eisen, who had made them for the members of the Hero Party during their journey as a way of expressing gratitude towards their efforts as warriors on their birthdays. Eisen also always made steaks for Stark's birthday. Stark recalls his brother making a steak for his birthday as well and that his brother was the one who told him to run and escape the fateful night of the demon attack. In better spirits, he enjoys the rest of his birthday with his companions.

## [LOCATIONS] Aufgabe Federation
The **Aufgabe Federation** ｢アオフガーベ連 (れん) 峰 (ぽう) , *Aofugābe Renpō*?｣ is a region situated in Imperial Territory.

## Overview]

Aufgabe Federation is a region that consists of a muddy forest and a village. It has two paths leading to the Imperial Capital, one being a mountain path and the other a main road that was constructed about a year after the death of Himmel the Hero. This region is located south of the Imperial Capital.

The village is of decent size. Before the construction of the main road, adventurers used to frequent the village. While the village does not have an inn, it does feature a vacant inn. Additionally, the village has its own fields and a bar.

## Synopsis]

### History]

Around twenty-nine years before the death of Himmel the Hero, a group of Shadow Warriors from the Empire received orders to monitor the mountain path in the Aufgabe Federation and eliminate all individuals on a provided list. 

Approximately thirty years later, construction began on the main road in the Aufgabe Federation, which would prevent people from using the mountain path. One of these Shadow Warriors, Radaal, would eventually become the mayor of the village.

### Imperial Territory Travels Arc]

Thirty-one years after the death of the Hero Himmel, Frieren's Party stops in a village within the Aufgabe Federation. Radaal, the village's elderly mayor, welcomes them and offers a vacant cabin so that they can rest. While the villagers speak kindly of him, Frieren is suspicious of Radaal's intentions, as she recognizes him as a hardened warrior.

That night, Radaal confronts the party. He first encounters Stark, who is standing guard at the door, and knocks him out. He then storms into the cabin and temporarily subdues Frieren. However, Stark and Fern quickly fight back, and Frieren ultimately holds Radaal at bay with her staff. She convinces him to abandon his mission since no one remembers it anymore. Subsequently, Frieren's Party leaves the village under the cover of night, leaving Radaal to reflect on his choices.

The next morning, Frieren's Party is seen traveling to the Imperial Capital along the main road, which is covered in thick mud.

## Inhabitants & Visitors]

### Inhabitants]

### Visitors]

- "Aufgabe" in German means "task" or "assignment", referring to something that needs to be done or completed.

- Viz Media localized "連峰" (Renpō) as "federation", although it typically means "mountain range".

## [LOCATIONS] Aureole
**Aureole** ｢魂の眠る地 (オレオール) , *Oreōru*?｣, also referred to as **The Land Where Souls Rest** ｢魂 (たましい) の眠 (ねむ) る地 (ち) , *Tamashī no nemuru chi*?｣ or **Heaven**, is a gathering location for souls. It is located in the northernmost end of the continent, Ende, where the Demon King's Castle is also based.

## Overview]

Located in the Northern Lands, Aureole is a place humans refer to as "heaven"; a place where one could meet with the souls of the dead. Recorded in the notes of Flamme, Aureole is where Flamme visited and spoke with her old comrades. Upon reading Flamme's notes of this encounter, traveling north to Aureole and reuniting with Himmel became Frieren's goal for her new journey.

Due to Aureole being considered as the heaven of the world, it is presumed that the Goddess of Creation resides there.

## History]

At some point in her life, Flamme journeyed to Aureole and spoke with her former comrades. She documented the encounter in her notes for Frieren to refer to a thousand years in the future, guarding the notes with a long-lasting protection spell.

## Synopsis]

After Himmel's death, Heiter and Eisen correspond over mail, and Heiter discovers the location of a real and existing record of Flamme's notes that includes details of her being able to communicate with the dead.

Frieren and Fern visit Eisen to provide any assistance for him, and he requests their aid in looking for the Great Mage Flamme's notes in the Voll Basin. During their search, Eisen explains that he felt pity for Frieren over her regret surrounding not getting to know Himmel more, and their quest to find the notes was to help her directly express to Himmel her thoughts. The group manages to locate a giant tree covering ruins, and Frieren removes the protective barrier that surrounds it. Inside, they find the notes, and the book opens up to the page detailing Flamme's visit to Aureole, where she described her meeting with the souls of her old comrades. With persuasion from Eisen, Frieren decides to make Aureole her destination for the possibility of speaking with Himmel once again.

During their travels through the Northern Lands, Frieren and her party encounters Kraft, an Elf with strong faith in the Goddess of Creation. When Frieren tells him about their intended journey to Aureole, Kraft mentions his wish to be praised by the Goddess in heaven when he passes.

## Inhabitants]

- Various souls

- Goddess of Creation (presumed)

## Visitors]

- Flamme

## Gallery]

Concept art by Seiko Yoshioka.

## [LOCATIONS] Bande Woods
The **Bande Woods** ｢バンデ森 (しん) 林 (りん) , *Bande Shinrin*?｣ is a dense forest situated in the Northern Lands.

## Overview]

### Terrain and Ecology]

The Bande Woods is a dense forest of mostly deciduous trees, some creeks, and wildlife, including herbs, fungi, and boar-like creatures. Dangerous monsters roam the area, including a bird-like monster that hunts by slamming prey into the ground. The wagon Frieren's Party travels in is hunted by this monster, forcing them to spend a few days on reparations.

## Synposis]

### Travels to Äußerst Arc]

Twenty-nine years after Himmel's death, Frieren's Party travel through the Bande Woods by catching a ride on a wagon with an accessory merchant. Frieren discusses the bracelet Stark bought for Fern for her birthday, which shares the same mirrored lotus flower design as a ring Himmel previously gifted Frieren. Their discussion is interrupted by an attack from a bird-like monster, who lifts their wagon in the air. Frieren jumps out of the wagon and blasts the monster in midair, dropping them to the ground and damaging the wagon in the process.

While the party repairs the wagon, Frieren realizes she has lost Himmel's ring. Meanwhile, Sein reveals that the mirrored lotus represents eternal love, much to Stark's dismay and Fern's annoyance at his reaction. After the wagon is fixed, Fern realizes that Frieren lost her ring and assists her in searching for it. With the aid of a spell for finding lost accessories from the merchant, Frieren locates the ring. As the party proceeds onwards through the woods, Frieren reflects on how she obtained the ring and that she is happy she did not give up on finding it.

## Inhabitants & Visitors]

### Visitors]

- Frieren

- Fern

- Stark

- Sein

- Accessory merchant

## Events]

- Frieren loses and then recovers the mirrored lotus ring that she received from Himmel.
Frieren receives the spell for finding lost accessories from the accessory merchant.

## Trivia]

- "Bande" is an out-of-use form of the word "binde." It is strongly related to the German word "band," meaning "band" or "bonds." In German, "bande" can refer to a "gang" or often a group of negative connotated people.

## [LOCATIONS] Bier Region
The **Bier Region** ｢ビーア地 (ち) 方 (ほう) , *Bīa Chihō*?｣ is a region situated in the Northern Plateau.

## Overview]

The Bier Region is one of the more populated areas of the Northern Plateau, featuring fertile lands ideal for agriculture. Notably, it hosts the only granary in the entire Northern Plateau.

### The Town]

The town is quite populated, especially considering its location within the dangerous Northern Plateau. It boasts numerous bars and, thanks to the granary and local brewing activities, is relatively prosperous. Various shops can also be found throughout the area.

### The Mine]

The mine that Fass dug after hearing a legend that claimed Boshaft was preserved somewhere nearby. His efforts led him to uncover a stone monument with an inscription in ancient elvish, which confirmed his beliefs.

#### Milliarde's Boshaft Stash]

A room containing Milliarde's stash of Boshaft within the mine is located near the original monument. The stash was uncovered by Fass after two hundred years of searching.

## Synopsis]

### History]

Over a millennium before the death of Himmel the Hero, Milliarde decides to kill some time and carves an inscription in the Bier Region that describes Boshaft as the finest spirit. She also places a storage full of Boshaft near the inscription, and places a powerful barrier over it.

### Continued Northern Travels Arc]

Twenty-nine years after Himmel's death, Frieren's Party travels through the Bier Region and stops in a town to stock up on supplies. While there, they meet Fass, who persuades Frieren to help him uncover Boshaft. He informs them about the inscription and the ruins he discovered. Although Frieren initially refuses to assist, even with the offer of twenty Reich gold coins, she later changes her mind, encouraged by Stark and Fern.

For the next three months, Frieren's Party stays in the town and successfully dispels the barrier. Once they open the door to the ruins and find Boshaft, Fass takes a sip. He struggles to describe the taste, prompting Frieren to declare it awful—worse than any alcohol she has ever encountered. Noticing that Stark hasn't tasted it yet, she forces him to take a sip. Stark reacts with shock at the terrible flavor, which leads to laughter among the party.

Fass reflects on the drink’s taste and laughs, claiming there is enough for everyone in the village to share. Later, Fass and the party are seen enjoying the drink with the rest of the villagers. Although Fass admits it was a disappointing outcome, he insists it was the most fun evening he's ever had. As they leave the town, he concludes that if one is going to drink, they might as well enjoy it to the fullest.

## Inhabitants & Visitors]

### Inhabitants]

### Visitors]

- With Frieren's aid, Fass ultimately finds Boshaft after a two-hundred year search.

## [LOCATIONS] Bohne Village
**Bohne Village** ｢ボーネ村 (むら) , *Bōne Mura*?｣ is a village located in Imperial Territory.

## Overview]

Bohne Village is a sizable human settlement, presumably situated near the checkpoint at Kino Pass. Surrounded by flatlands and bordered by forests, it also has mountainous areas nearby. During the Liberation Festival, the village becomes a lively hub with various stalls offering a wide range of food. It is home to numerous houses and buildings, including a bell tower, possibly part of a church. In the village square stands a statue of Himmel the Hero.

## Synopsis]

### History]

More than seven years into the Hero Party's journey, Himmel defeated a 10-meter-long serpent near Bohne Village.

After the defeat of the Demon King, the Hero Party passed through Bohne Village on their return to the Royal Capital. While in the village, they overheard a story that exaggerated the serpent's size, turning the 10-meter creature Himmel had slain into a 100-meter-long beast.

### Imperial Territory Travels Arc]

Thirty-one years after the death of Himmel the Hero, Frieren's Party arrives in Bohne Village during the Liberation Festival, a celebration marking the anniversary of the Demon King's defeat. The village mayor invites Frieren, Fern, and Stark to stay for the festivities.

During the festival, they visit a statue of Himmel, which is believed to bring good luck if touched. Upon arrival, they notice that the statue has been completely altered. Frieren explains that this is typical in Imperial Territory, where the Empire often deifies deceased heroes. Though Stark feels uneasy about the changes, Frieren reassures him that the villagers mean no harm and sincerely revere Himmel.

After the festival ends, Frieren's Party continues their journey to Aureole.

## Inhabitants & Visitors]

## [LOCATIONS] Bredt Region
The **Bredt Region** ｢ブレット地 (ち) 方 (ほう) , *Buretto Chihō*?｣ is a region situated in the Central Lands. It contains farmlands and forests, as well as the Voll Basin where the Great Mage Flamme's notes are hidden. It is also where Eisen lives.

## Overview]

The Bredt Region is located in the Central Lands with farmlands and forests. It is in close vicinity to the Northern Lands, and the Voll Basin is located within the region.

### Terrain and Ecology]

The region is surrounded by ridges and contains some settlements. On the central plane grows the deep forest, which is where the notes of the Great Mage Flamme are supposedly hidden. There are different geological features, with the Voll Basin being the most notable, and it provides habitats for multiple species. Humans settle the area and use it for farmlands. Within the Voll Basin is a deep forest, featuring mixed woods, where wildlife like lizards and grapes can be found. A peculiarity is the huge, thousand-year-old tree enhanced under protective magic, which Flamme planted as a guardian of her dwelling.

### Eisen's House]

Eisen's house is a small, wooden cabin in the region . It is a house with a single room, windows, a table with multiple chairs, a drawer, and a bed. Outside of the house lies the graves of Eisen's family, who were killed in a demon attack.

### Voll Basin]

#### The Deep Forest]

A wooded area in the Voll Basin of the Bredt Region where the notes of the Great Mage Flamme are supposedly hidden.

#### Ruins]

A building within the deep forest of the Voll Basin, which houses the notes of the Great Mage Flamme. A tree planted over a thousand years ago by Flamme and Frieren has grown over it.

## Synopsis]

### History]

At some point during Frieren's mentorship under Flamme, Flamme planted a tree that she intended to act as the guardian of a building, which in the present has been reduced to ruins. Frieren commented that the tree did not appear to be a reliable guardian, to which Flamme responded that it will protect the place for more than a millennium once it fully grows. Frieren replied that by then, Flamme will be dead. Flamme advised Frieren that Frieren herself won't be dead, and one day when Frieren makes a grave mistake, what Flamme left behind will guide her.

During the Hero Party's journey to defeat the Demon King, they visited Eisen's house in the region, which contained two graves that turned out to be Eisen's family. Heiter proceeded to pray for Eisen's family, and the party discussed Heiter's belief in Heaven's existence, which both Eisen and Frieren are skeptic about. Frieren mentioned that since magic is not yet capable of visualizing the souls of the deceased, the idea of Heaven cannot be proven. Himmel responded that he does not mind either way, a sentiment that Heiter agrees with, to Himmel's confusion. Heiter explained that even if Heaven does not exist, then he will still believe it does, because he would prefer it for those who struggled so hard to live. Himmel voiced his agreement, and the Hero Party then pray for Eisen's family.

At some point after the journey of the Hero Party and around three years before Frieren and Fern come to visit Eisen takes in Stark making him his apprentice. Eisen teaches him his technique. After an event where Eisen hits Stark, the boy leaves to end up in the Riegel Canyon.

### Beyond Journey's End Arc]

Twenty-eight years after the Himmel's death, Frieren and Fern travel to the Bredt Region. They visit Eisen at his house, where he can be seen praying near the graves of his family. As they chat and catch up on each others' lives, Eisen is surprised to see that Frieren has taken in an apprentice, and Frieren learns that Eisen and Heiter had been exchanging letters.

Afterwards, they start traveling to the Voll Basin, which is supposedly where the notes of the Great Mage Flamme reside, as discovered by Heiter in his research. Frieren directs them to look for a large tree, an effort which takes them at least a day. Underneath the tree from 1000 years ago are ruins, which contain the notes of Flamme. They retrieve the notes, and Frieren also reveals that she was an apprentice of Flamme.

Within the notes, Flamme reveals that Heaven does, in fact, exist at a location called Aureole, the place where souls rest in the northernmost part of the continent. Frieren realizes that Aureole will therefore be within Ende, where the Demon King's Castle also stands. Eisen asks Frieren to go to Aureole and talk to Himmel. Frieren agrees to this, though she is discouraged by the frigid temperatures in the north.

While on the way back to his house, Eisen asks Fern if Frieren is a good teacher, which she is initially unsure about. However, she eventually responds that despite Frieren's flaws, Frieren has been trying to understand her, and thus she considers Frieren a good teacher.

The carriage later drops them off at Eisen's house, and Frieren voices her surprise that Eisen is choosing not go on the journey with them, to which he maintains that he will be nothing but a burden. Frieren and Fern decide they will use the same path the Hero Party took, which will take then ten years. They then depart for their adventure.

## [LOCATIONS] Decke Region
The **Decke Region** ｢デッケ地 (ち) 方 (ほう) , *Dekke Chihō*?｣ is a snowy, mountainous region in the Northern Lands. It has occasional snowstorms that can be quite deadly without any shelter.

## Overview]

### Terrain and Ecology]

The Decke Region is located near the Schwer Mountains in the Northern Lands, and it has rough, mountainous terrain and forests with snowstorms. Due to its elevated altitude, the onset of cold and snowy seasonal weather in winter is early and lasts long. The area becomes dangerous without shelter.

The vegetation within the region is sparse, and, due to the snowstorms, they are frequently covered under snow. The forests consist of coniferous trees. There appears to be no human occupation or usage of the land besides a lone cabin. Many wildlife species can be found, such as hare-like and fox-like creatures and a form of seed rats adapted to the location. In the forest, typical foraged foods like berries and nuts can be gathered. As with most places in the Northern Lands, travelers may encounter dangerous creatures.

### Cabin]

A small, one-room cabin is located within the Decke Region at the foot of the mountains. It is used by adventurers as a shelter in the event of a snowstorm. It is visited by Frieren in her travels during the fifty years between the two Era Meteors she watches with the Hero Party and by Frieren's Party and Kraft when they are stranded for half a year by the winter weather. It appears to be regularly maintained.

### The Forest]

A forest in the Decke Region hosts wildlife that has adapted to the harsh seasonal conditions in the region.

## Synopsis]

### History]

Frieren travels through the Decke Region in the fifty years between the Era Meteors that she watches with the Hero Party. She stays in the small cabin at the foot of the mountains. 

### Travels to Äußerst Arc]

Twenty-eight years after Himmel's death, Frieren's Party travel to the Decke Region. Stark collapses and there is a heavy snowstorm, so they seek shelter in a cabin Frieren remembers was there eighty years ago. As they open the door, they see an elf doing squats inside, and quickly close the door. Fern protests staying in the cabin and asks Frieren to find another place, but before they can, the elf opens the door and asks Frieren if she is an elf.

Inside the cabin, the elf, who is named Kraft, has a conversation with Frieren about the rarity of encountering another elf. Due to Stark's low body temperature, Kraft helps warm him up by sleeping with him, leading to Stark waking up in confusion. After the misunderstanding is settled, Stark compliments Kraft on his build. 

Due to the current condition of the weather, the four of them stay in the cabin. To survive, they gather supplies from Kraft's wagon, hunt, and forage for food during the stay. They share their meals together and Kraft teaches Fern and Stark various things. One day, while in the forest, Kraft and Frieren have a discussion on the Goddess of Creation, spurred by Kraft asking Frieren to give a necklace to Fern for her strong devotion. 

Months later, once the winter has passed and the mountain is traversable again, Frieren's party and Kraft part ways as they continue their separate adventures.

## Visitors]

- Frieren

- Fern

- Stark

- Kraft

## Events]

- Frieren stays in the cabin during her travels between the Era Meteors.

- Frieren's Party spends the winter with Kraft in the cabin in the Decke Region.
During their stay, the twenty-eighth year after the Hero Himmel's passing ends, and the twenty-ninth year begins.

## [LOCATIONS] Drachen Region
The **Drachen Region** ｢ドラッへ地 (ち) 方 (ほう) , *Dorahhe Chihō*?｣ is a region situated in the Northern Plateau.

## Overview]

The Drachen Region is a rugged area covered with forests. It is home to a human settlement, as well as cliffs and chasms. Like in the rest of the Northern Plateau, dragons typically travel in a thunder and are known to nest in this region.

### The Village]

The village is a relatively large settlement, though it is economically impoverished. Following an attack by a thunder of dragons, many buildings were left in ruins, prompting ongoing reconstruction efforts. The village also features a church that serves as a place for healing.

## Synopsis]

### The Golden Land Arc]

Thirty years after the death of the Hero Himmel, Frieren's Party encounters a village in the Drachen Region that has been devastated by a dragon attack. Drachen Region chief explains that they were assaulted by a thunder of dragons and request Frieren to exterminate the nearby nesting dragons.

At first, Frieren refuses, stating that the village is beyond saving. However, after Fern and Stark challenge her decision, and the villager offers a reward—a spell that allows you to say tongue twisters without tripping over your words—she changes her mind.

Frieren and her party trace the dragons' mana, searching the region for their nest. After locating it, they engage in battle and successfully defeat the thunder of dragons. Upon returning to the village, they seek healing at a nearby church and receive their reward.

Later, as the party continues their journey, Fern asks Frieren why she always requests rewards for helping others. Frieren explains that Himmel once taught her to accept small rewards to avoid leaving people feeling indebted.

## Inhabitants & Visitors]

### Inhabitants]

### Visitors]

- Fern

## Events]

- Frieren's Party defeats a thunder of dragons.

## Trivia]

- "Drachen" is German for "dragons", referring to mythical, often fire-breathing creatures that appear in various legends and stories.

The National Foundation Festival is held in Eiseberg, and was originally meant to be a social season for aristocracy. Eiseberg is the base of operations of the Magic Special Forces, the Shadow Warriors, and the Court of the Sacred Staff.

## [LOCATIONS] Empire
**This article is a stub.**

*You can help Frieren Wiki by **expanding it**. Please be sure to adhere to the Editor's Guidelines, Manual of Style, and Image Policy.*

The **Empire** ｢帝 (てい) 国 (こく) , *Teikoku*?｣ is a country in the Northern Lands that once united the majority of the continent. Its capital is Eiseberg.

## Overview]

### Eiseberg]

*Main article: Eiseberg*

## History]

The Empire was once the largest human nation on the continent, having been around during the time of the early days of the Demon King when his armies freely marauded across the land and warred with humanity without restrain. Like a majority of human society during this time, the Empire did not think highly of magic as a whole due to the influence, excessive usage, and extreme mastery of it by Demons to kill and terrorize humanity. As such, all forms of magic were deemed to be demonic techniques, and thus, open research on these techniques was considered taboo.

However, Flamme, a human mage and former apprentice of the immensely powerful mage Serie, was able to influence the Emperor to approve the research of magic country-wide, and she helped establish and educate a new division of Imperial Mages. Flamme was thus responsible for helping to usher in an era in which all of mankind would be able to use magic and acquire the power to oppose the Demon King's army. For this, Flamme is known as the founder of mankind's magic.

Due to Flamme's contributions, the Empire flourished and evolved its magic, which became integrated as an everyday aspect of the Empire's way of life. The Empire developed and increased their military prowess by applying magic to their armies and continued to expand and research magic for military purposes for the next few centuries, building legions of trained mages with enough power to topple entire countries. To counteract any possibility of rebellion and uprising by these powerful mages, secret anti-magic units were established, with the Magic Special Forces being one unit officially acknowledged by the Empire. Other rumored units included the Shadow Warriors and the Court of the Sacred Staff.

## Synopsis]

## [LOCATIONS] Ende
**Ende** ｢エンデ, *Ende*?｣ is a cold region located at the northernmost tip of the continent. It holds the current Demon King's Castle and is also the alleged location of Aureole, a place regarded as heaven or the afterlife where souls rest.

## Overview]

### Demon King's Castle]

*Main article: Demon King's Castle*
The Hero Party traveled to Ende in order to confront the Demon King in his castle. The journey to reach the castle is described as a long journey where many things happened.

### Aureole]

*Main article: Aureole*
According to the Great Mage Flamme, Aureole, also known as The Land Where Souls Rest or Heaven, is said to be located in Ende. When Flamme visits Aureole, she is able to speak with the souls of her departed friends. Reaching Aureole is the goal of Frieren's current party.

## Inhabitants]

- Demon King

## Visitors]

- Frieren

- Eisen

- Heiter

- Himmel

- Flamme

## Events]

- Flamme travels to Aureole and speaks to the souls of her departed friends. Her notes about this event are stored in the Voll Basin.

- The Hero Party travels to the Demon King's Castle in Ende and defeat the Demon King, ushering in the Era of Peace.

## Trivia]

- "Ende" is German for "end / ending."

## [LOCATIONS] Eng Road (Locality)
The **Eng Road** ｢エング街 (かい) 道 (どう) , *Engu Kaidō*?｣ is a passageway that is commonly used for merchants traveling in the Northern Lands. It leads to a fairly developed town, which has a festival in honor of the Hero Party liberating it.

## Overview]

### Terrain and Ecology]

The region around the Eng Road is a terrain with mountains and steep hills in the Northern Lands, which can lead to landslides that end up blocking the path. The forest within the valleys has mixed species of trees, and the elevated areas grow coniferous trees. Merchants appear to bring in goods through the Eng Road and into the nearby town. The area was once attacked by a demon, but it was vanquished by the Hero Party.

### The Town]

A fairly developed town can be reached through the Eng Road, and the road is used by merchants wanting to sell and trade in the town. It is well protected, with walls surrounding the town. Every year, it has a liberation festival in honor of the Hero Party subduing a demon. The residents celebrate by decorating a statue of the Hero Party and engaging in festivities.

## Synopsis]

### History]

The Hero Party defeated a two-legged monster with multiple snake heads and liberated the region around the Eng Road.

### Beyond Journey's End Arc]

Twenty-eight years after Himmel's passing, Frieren, Fern, and Stark arrive at a portion of the Eng Road blocked from a landslide. After helping a merchant by clearing the road, they travel with him to town. When they reach the town, they find out the Liberation Festival is taking place that same night, which commemorates the day the Hero Party subjugated the monster that was oppressing the region. The townspeople celebrate by decorating the statues of the Hero Party. The merchant tells Frieren that it is on this day everyone remembers Himmel and his party, making her recall a memory of when Himmel told her he makes statues of himself and the party so that Frieren would not be alone in the future. They reach the town and see the statues decorated with flowers and the residents celebrating. The next day, the trio continues their voyage towards Heaven.

## Inhabitants & Visitors]

### Inhabitants]

- Demon with snake heads (*formerly*)

### Visitors]

- Eng Road merchant

- Frieren

- Fern

- Stark

## Events]

- Frieren's Party clear a landslide on the Eng Road.

- The trio visit the liberation festival held in the Eng Road town to commemorate the Hero Party.

## [LOCATIONS] Ernst Region
The **Ernst Region** ｢エルンスト地 (ち) 方 (ほう) , *Erunsto Chihō*?｣ is a region situated in the Northern Plateau.

## Overview]

The Ernst Region is primarily composed of grasslands and has a cold climate. It is an agricultural area capable of producing a variety of crops. The region is known for being a peaceful area, featuring a well-maintained main road and almost no dangerous monsters. This has made it a key passage connecting the Northern Plateau to the Empire, lying adjacent to the Wissen Mountains. A farm village is also located within the region.

Due to its close proximity to the Empire, the Ernst Region is strongly influenced by the largest country in the Northern Lands. The frequent travel between the two areas leads to cultural overlap and creates ambiguity regarding control over the region between the Chivalric Order of Norm and the Empire.

### The Farm Village]

The farm village is a sizable human settlement with its own agricultural fields. It also includes an inn and a cabin that houses various grimoires.

## Synopsis]

### Goddess's Monument Arc]

Thirty-one years after the death of the Hero Himmel, Frieren's Party travels through the Ernst Region and decides to stay at an inn in a farming village. The innkeeper approaches them for assistance, as a monster with metal-like hardness has devastated their crops. In exchange, Frieren requests a grimoire of her choosing.

While observing the fields at night, Frieren, Fern, and Stark discover that the monster is an ancient Golem from the era of the Unified Empire. Frieren successfully deactivates it and informs the innkeeper the next day that she can contact the Empire to collect the Golem, as it could be valuable if properly maintained. As a reward, Frieren receives a spell that allows a paper airplane to fly far.

## Inhabitants & Visitors]

### Inhabitants]

- Ernst Region innkeeper

### Visitors]

- Stark

- Frieren

- Fern

## Events]

- Frieren's Party discovers an ancient Golem from the era of the Unified Empire.

## Gallery]

### Manga]

Ernst Region.

## Trivia]

- "Ernst" is German for "seriousness" or "earnestness", denoting a state of being serious or a focus on important matters.

## [LOCATIONS] Etwas Mountains
The **Etwas Mountains** ｢エトヴァス山 (さん) 地 (ち) , *Etovasu Sanchi*?｣ are a mountainous region situated in the Northern Lands. It lies in what was once a volcanic area. In the past, the mountains were known for their hot springs and attracted many adventurers.

## Overview]

The Etwas Mountains are located in the Northern Lands, in a volcanic area where eruptions once occurred, though none have happened for centuries. Due to this inactivity and the region's warmer climate, the Etwas Mountains were once famous for their hot springs, which attracted many adventurers. However, the hot springs dried up at some point before the death of Himmel the Hero, causing adventurers to stop visiting. As a result, the area's inhabitants left, and the villages were abandoned.

## Synopsis]

### History]

During their journey to defeat the Demon King, the Hero Party passed through the Etwas Mountains and a village where they experienced the region's hot springs. While there, they sought the secret hot spring of the Etwas Mountains, which required them to traverse the territory of a monster. This journey was particularly challenging, with both Frieren and Eisen wanting to turn back. Upon finding the hot spring, they discovered it was merely a foot bath. Nevertheless, they sat and enjoyed the view of the mountains before leaving.

### Continued Northern Travels Arc]

Twenty-nine years after the death of Himmel the Hero, Frieren's Party travels through the Etwas Mountains in search of the old village that Frieren visited. They find only a single cabin, which worries Frieren. A resident of the cabin informs them that the village was abandoned over thirty years ago, and that the only remaining hot spring may be the secret hot spring of the Etwas Mountains. This prompts Frieren to consider departing for the next town, but Stark convinces her to search for the secret hot spring instead. 

 
While on their journey to find it, they enter the territory of a three-headed dragon and manage to fend it off. When they finally locate the hot spring, Stark and Fern discover that the water is shallow. Frieren explains that this is why she was hesitant to search for it. Despite this, Stark decides to enter the spring anyway and encourages them to join him. As they relax in the secret hot spring, Stark reveals that he heard about this place from his master, who told him that the journey was not worth the effort, though he cherished the memory and would never forget the view from that day.

On their way back, Fern comments on how the return journey is just as harsh, and Stark remarks that perhaps it was not worth it after all.

## Inhabitants & Visitors]

### Inhabitants]

- Etwas Mountains family

### Visitors]

- Frieren

- Fern

- Stark

- Himmel

- Heiter

- Eisen

## Events]

- Frieren, Fern and Stark find the secret hot spring of the Etwas Mountains.

## [LOCATIONS] Fabel Village
**Fabel Village** ｢ファーベル村 (むら) , *Fāberu Mura*?｣ is a village located in the Northern Lands.

## Overview]

Fabel Village is a village situated in a forested area of the Northern Lands. The village has on one side fields for crops adjacent to it, and on the other, it is situated beside tall hills with near-vertical slopes. The inhabitants raise animals like geese. In the village's plaza, there is a statue of the Hero of the South. The plaza also serves as a venue for community events where acts like puppet theater performances, which depict the battle between the Hero of the South and Schlacht the Omniscient, can take place.

 

## Synopsis]

### History]

Many years ago, during the war against the Demon King, the Hero of the South liberated Fabel Village from the Demon armies and the Seven Sages of Destruction. Fabel Village was one of many villages freed by the Hero during his one year-long campaign, which ended with his death at the hands of Schlacht the Omniscient and the Sages. Although the Hero of the South did not defeat the Demon King, the faith in him within Fabel Village remains strong. The absence of his corpse has led to legends that he continues to fight against Schlacht the Omniscient to the present day.

### Continued Northern Travels Arc]

Twenty-nine years after the death of Himmel the Hero, Frieren and her party receive a request from the Chief of Fabel Village to clean the statue of the village's Hero. Frieren agrees after being offered a spell to scratch the itchy parts on your back". As Stark prepares to polish the statue, expecting another statue of Himmel, he is shocked to find a statue of a middle-aged man. 

Frieren then explains to Fern and Stark that the statue depicts the Hero of the South. She elaborates that many heroes challenged the Demon King, and among them, the Hero of the South was said to have been the strongest Hero of humanity. Stark initially thinks this sounds exaggerated, but Frieren assures him it is not, emphasizing that he deserved that title.

Frieren recounts that during the long war against the Demon King, the Hero of the South made significant progress, as within a single year, he destroyed the frontline forces of the Demon King and advanced to the northernmost end of the Northern Plateau, which served as the central supply route for the Demon King's army. It was here that he was besieged by Schlacht the Omniscient and all of the Seven Sages of Destruction, leading to his demise, though he managed to slay Schlacht and three of the Sages before falling. 

After Frieren concludes her tale, they clean the statue of the Hero of the South and receive their reward from the village chief. Soon after, villagers gather around the newly polished statue as Frieren and her party watch contentedly.

## Inhabitants & Visitors]

### Inhabitants]

- Chief of Fabel Village

### Visitors]

- Stark

- Frieren

- Fern

- Hero of the South

## Events]

- The Hero of the South liberates Fabel Village and other surrounding villages from the Seven Sages of Destruction.

- Frieren describes the story of the Hero of the South to Fern and Stark.

## [LOCATIONS] Farbe Region
The **Farbe Region** ｢ファルベ地 (ち) 方 (ほう) , *Farube Chihō*?｣ is a region situated in Imperial Territory.

## Overview]

The Farbe Region is situated in the Empire and is characterized by its forested landscape. It features a main road frequented by merchants, along with various farms and a village. The region is home to monsters, particularly in the forests, which often create problems for travelers on the road. Additionally, a shed once stood along the main road but was destroyed by monsters.

Although the village in the region is not wealthy, it does feature an altered statue of the Great Mage Flamme, represented as an old man, in an open area.

## Synopsis]

### Imperial Territory Travels Arc]

Thirty-one years after the death of Himmel the Hero, Frieren's Party travels through the Farbe Region. A woman from a nearby village asks for their help to deal with local monsters after the imperial patrol failed to respond to the villagers’s request. In exchange, she offers a vase said to induce nightmares, which Frieren accepts.

While searching the area, Frieren, Fern, and Stark are ambushed by monsters in the forest. After a grueling fight, they defeat the creatures and later find the corpses of the imperial patrol, massacred by the same monsters.

They then return to the village, explain what happened, and receive their reward. That night, while camping, Frieren decides to test the vase by trying to sleep with it, surprising Fern and Stark with her boldness.

## [LOCATIONS] Graf Dach's Domain
**Graf Dach's Domain** ｢ダッハ伯 (はく) 爵 (しゃく) 領 (りよう) , *Dahha Hakushaku-ryō*?｣ is a holding under the rule of nobleman Graf Dach, located in the Northern Lands. Its seat of power lies in a large, fortified town.

## Overview]

The main town in Graf Dach's Domain is large and well-developed, featuring numerous houses, shops, magic shops, and inns. The settlement also serves as the center of Graf Dach's rule, housing his castle with defensive wall and towers. Surrounding the town are several areas under Graf Dach's control, including at least one village, a large forest, and a flowing river. Snakes inhabit these areas as well.

 

### The castle]

Graf Dach's castle has several floors featuring numerous rooms, like a big dining hall and includes a stable for horses and a coach. In a separate room on a stand with the coat of arms, with a sword over mountains on a blue ground behind it, the Dach's family's treasured heirloom, the sword that once belonged to a prominent demon, is kept.

## Synopsis]

### History]

During their quest to subjugate the Demon King, the Hero Party passed through Graf Dach's Domain and met the great-grandfather of the current Graf Dach, who ruled at that time. The Graf tasked the party with recovering the family's treasured heirloom sword, which once belonged to a notable demon. The Dach family, known for their assertiveness, often made unreasonable requests, and the noble threatened the Hero Party with execution if they failed to return the sword. The party then had to travel back to the Schwer Mountains to recover it. In return for their efforts, they were handsomely rewarded with money.

### Continued Northern Travels Arc]

Twenty-nine years after the passing of Himmel the Hero, Frieren and her party pass through the largest town in Graf Dach's Domain. Stark comments on how long it has been since they visited such a large settlement, while Frieren wishes to leave as soon as possible, much to the surprise of both Stark and Fern.

Shortly after, the party is invited to dinner by Graf Dach, which Frieren reluctantly agrees to attend. At the banquet, Graf Dach promptly requests their help in retrieving the family heirloom sword, which has been stolen by a demon, with Frieren noting that the same happened to his great-grandfather. Frieren agrees in exchange for a grimoire as a reward.

Frieren and her companions search through a nearby forest and come across an abandoned village. There, they meet a priestess who claims to have buried the villagers killed by a demon. However, Frieren uncovers that the graves are empty, revealing the priestess as the demon who stole Graf Dach's sword. The party swiftly defeats the demon. Afterwards, they pay their respects to the fallen villagers and offer prayers for them.

Upon their return to Graf Dach's castle, they hand over the heirloom sword and claim their promised reward. As they leave the town, Stark asks Frieren about the spell in the grimoire, to which she replies that it teaches a spell to turn a red apple to a green apple.

## Inhabitants & Visitors]
